< review>
I have long enjoyed the Togo's variety of sandwich offerings.  Though there are also other menu items like soups and salads, the sandwiches are what I enjoy most.  To me, their pastrami(or #9, as it is mostly known), is the best and beyond comparison anywhere else!  The recent pairing of Togo's locations, under the same roof with Baskin Robbins ice cream, is a very smart, yet logical concept.  It allows patrons to enjoy either food venue by itself, or in combination.  Pricing is on par with similar sandwich shops like Subway, and offers the occasional featured sandwich items as well.  Definitely worth the food dining experience, in my opinion.</review>

< review>
This was one of the best haircare services I've received in the 5+ years of living in Southern California.

Mino Salon (Master Stylist) is a gem of a find. I called the salon and Mino himself picked up right away. He was friendly, professional and incredibly accommodating from directing me to their private parking lot, consulting me on my haircut and color while personable and demonstrating a technical mastery in the way he communicates. The consultation he gives is honest and he is transparent about the cost breakdown

I was really worried about finding a good salon amidst the pandemic but was pleasantly surprised and comforted by the safety standards set in place. At most there was only two people in the salon at one time, everyone wore masks the entirety of the service, everyone's temperature was taken who walked through the door and the seats were sanitized after every use.

Mino did my haircut and Avi did my color. He was very attentive, made suggestions and gave me exactly the haircut I wanted. Avi was incredibly detailed and accommodating with the color, taking the time to make sure it was its best.

If you need a quality, safe, personable and professional service for your hair- look no further! I'm very happy with the results.<//review>

< review>
It really pains me to write this review, but I feel the need to warn other customers about this salon after my absolutely traumatic and horrible experience there. I trusted the glowing reviews for Mino online and gave him a try after not having a haircut for almost a year due to quarantine. I went into the salon with long, thick wavy hair down to my waist. I routinely receive many compliments on my long hair, so I made very clear to Mino that I wanted to keep it on the longer side, but cut as much as would allow me to still wear it in a high ponytail. I lifted my hair into a high ponytail to show him the length I wanted. It would come to about mid-back or chest area. Then suddenly, without warning, Mino HACKED OFF ALL MY HAIR in one motion. He just sawed it off at shoulder length, and then quickly ran into the back of the salon holding my hair in his hands. I was in such shock and immediately demanded to know why he had done this.

He had many excuses, but ultimately admitted that he made a mistake. But since he kept my hair, my suspicion is that he will sell my very long thick hair for money, since virgin hair (never chemically treated or dyed) of that length and thickness can be sold for hundreds of dollars to make wigs. My hair ended up being chin-length when blow-dried, but even shorter when airdried. I feel violated and robbed of my beautiful long hair that took me years to grow.

I will also add that this salon is NOT following pandemic protocols. When I made the appointment, Mino said I would be the only client in the salon, but when I arrived, there were a total of 8 people packed into the small space, and one of the customers was not wearing a mask. The salon looked very dirty and Mino didn't disinfect any surfaces before seating me in the chair that was just occupied by someone else. I should have left right then and there, but I felt guilty and wanted to be polite.

In the end, Mino offered to not charge me for my haircut, but I refused his offer and still paid for it, because I don't want him to think that he "made it right" somehow. It can't be made right until the hair grows back, which will take a long time. I'm sure Mino will deny my suspicion that he sold my hair, but I have no trust in anything he says after what happened to me in his salon.<//review>

This is a story about a young man and his everlasting journey to acquire his drivers licence. On the morning of Wednesday October 12th a man by the name of Louis arrived at my house and took me on a journey to practice my driving skills and see how I can improve on my ability to drive a vehicle from one point to another.
